phalatvAchchAnandasya pR^ithaguktiH | anubhUyamAnAnanda syAchchatAhetutvAdvAj~nAnasya pR^ithaguktiriti sarvamavadAtamityasheShamatimaN^galam.h || nArAyaNAchAryamukhendu
